   window.addEventListener('message',function(e) {

    toCamel = function( $str ) {
        return $str.toLowerCase().replace( /([^a-z0-9])/ig, ' ' ).trim().replace( /([ ][a-z])/ig, function( $1 ) {
            return $1.toUpperCase().trim();
        } ).replace( /\s*/ig, '' );
    };

// Turn query string items into an object with camel case names and merged duplicate key values
location.search.substring( 1 ).replace( /([^=&]+)(=([^&]*))?/g, function( matches, key, ignore, value ) {
    key = toCamel( decodeURIComponent( key ) );
    value = value !== undefined ? decodeURIComponent( value ) : '';

    query[ key ] === undefined ? query[ key ] = value : (typeof query[ key ].push === 'function' ? query[ key ].push( value ) : query[ key ] = [query[ key ], value]);
} );

        }
    }
    console.log("TP: Theme External fired");
}

           </a>
          </h2>
         </header>
         <div class="excerpt">
          <p>
